@resolution_weight_hated = 3
@resolution_weight_disliked = 4
@resolution_weight_unpopular = 5
@resolution_weight_normal = 6
@resolution_weight_popular = 6.5
@resolution_weight_loved = 7

@resolution_cost_t1 = 100
@resolution_cost_t2 = 150
@resolution_cost_t3 = 200
@resolution_cost_t4 = 250
@resolution_cost_t5 = 300
@resolution_cost_denounce = 25

@resolution_flag_timer = 360

#example_resolution = {
#	icon = "name of the icon key"
#	resources = {} # cost and category
#	target = yes/no # if this resolution requires a target country
#	harmful = yes/no # if the AI should consider this harmful when choosing target
#	modifier = {} # modifier to be applied to all community members if passed
#	triggered_modifier = {} # triggered modifier to be applied, scope is country
#	effect = {} # effect to be applied if passed, scope is proposer unless there is a target country - then scope is target country, with proposer in from scope
#	fail_effects = {} # effect to be applied if failed, scope is proposer unless there is a target country - then scope is target country, with proposer in from scope
#	potential = {} # potential trigger, scope is country
#	allow = {} # allow trigger, scope is country
#	active = {} # Enacted sesolutions are cancelled if this trigger fails
#	ai_weight = {} # ai weight modifiers, scope is country
#	valid_target = {} # valid targets trigger, scope is country
#}

# NOTE: Remember to add Resolutions to a Resolution Category!

# Galactic Market Resolutions
resolution_galactic_market_form = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_form_galactic_market"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_galactic_market_form_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			# Kickoff the Forming the Market event chain
			country_event = { id = action.96 }

			set_global_flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed

			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	modifier = {
		country_resource_max_add = 10000
	}

	potential = {
		NOR = {
			has_global_flag = galactic_market_founded
			has_global_flag = ongoing_market_nomination
		}

		is_gestalt = no
		is_homicidal = no
		count_diplo_ties = {
			limit = {
				OR = { is_country_type = default is_country_type = ascended_empire is_country_type = lost_empire }
				is_homicidal = no
			}
			count >= 3
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_popular

		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			is_auth_corporate = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			OR = {
				has_ai_personality = peaceful_traders
				has_ai_personality = ruthless_capitalists
			}
		}
		
		# wants access to rare resources
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			NOR = {
				has_monthly_income = { resource = volatile_motes value < 1 }
				has_monthly_income = { resource = rare_crystals value < 1 }
				has_monthly_income = { resource = exotic_gases value < 1 }
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				has_monthly_income = { resource = volatile_motes value < 1 }
				has_monthly_income = { resource = rare_crystals value < 1 }
				has_monthly_income = { resource = exotic_gases value < 1 }
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_xenophile = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_materialist = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_xenophobic_isolationists = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_valid_civic = civic_shared_burden
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_slaver_guilds = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_xenophobe = yes
			is_materialist = no
			is_auth_corporate = no
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_xenophobe = yes
			OR = {
				is_materialist = yes
				is_auth_corporate = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			years_passed > 50
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			years_passed > 100
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			years_passed > 150
		}
	}
}

# Ecology

resolution_ecology_repeal_1 = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_blue"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_ecology_repeal_1_effect_success

		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_ecology_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_ecology_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_ecology_recycling_initiatives"
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_unpopular
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_xenophile = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_xenophobe = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_civic_environmentalist = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner_species = { has_trait = eco_trait_clean }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			owner_species = { has_trait = eco_trait_dirty }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			count_country = {
				count < 4
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					relative_power = { who = prev category = economy value >= equivalent }
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			any_relation = {
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_rival = prev
					is_at_war_with = prev
				}
				count_country = {
					count < 4
					limit = {
						is_galactic_community_member = yes
						relative_power = { who = prev category = economy value >= equivalent }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_auth_corporate = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_valid_civic = civic_agribusiness
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			is_civic_mining_guilds = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			country_uses_food = no
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_lithoid_empire = yes
		}
	}
}

			is_civic_mining_guilds = no

		}

			any_relation = {
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {

				}

					count < 4
					limit = {

			is_civic_environmentalist = no

				count < 4
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					relative_power = { who = prev category = economy value >= equivalent }
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_relation = {
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_rival = prev
					is_at_war_with = prev
				}
				count_country = {
					count < 4
					limit = {
						is_galactic_community_member = yes
						relative_power = { who = prev category = economy value >= equivalent }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			has_valid_civic = civic_starvation_fearing
			is_lithoid_empire = no
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_valid_civic = civic_starvation_fearing
			is_lithoid_empire = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			has_valid_civic = civic_idealistic_foundation
		}

		modifier = {

			is_lithoid_empire = no
			has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_lithoid_empire = no
			has_valid_civic = civic_agribusiness
		}

			is_lithoid_empire = no

				has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
				has_valid_civic = civic_agribusiness
			}
			OR = {
				is_xenophile = yes
				is_spiritualist = yes
				is_pacifist = yes
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				has_ascension_perk = ap_arcology_project
				has_origin = origin_machine
				has_origin = origin_terraformer
			}
			NOR = {
				has_ascension_perk = ap_world_shaper
				is_civic_environmentalist = yes
				has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
				has_origin = origin_life_seeded
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_civic_functional_architecture = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				is_civic_mining_guilds = yes
				country_uses_food = no
				is_lithoid_empire = yes
				is_auth_corporate = yes
			}
		}

			is_militarist = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_lithoid_empire = yes

			factor = 1.2
			owner_species = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = trait_nonadaptive
					has_trait = trait_endemic
				}
			}
		}

			factor = 1.25
			country_uses_food = yes

		}
		modifier = {

resolution_ecology_paradise_initiative = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_ecolgical_protection"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t5
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 5

	modifier = {
		resolution_ecology_recycling_initiatives = 1
		resolution_ecology_natural_sanctuaries = 1
		resolution_ecology_integrated_gardens = 1
		resolution_ecology_environmental_control_board = 1
		resolution_ecology_paradise_initiative = 1
	}

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_paradise_initiative_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = ecology_pops_patch_flag }
			custom_tooltip = resolution_ecology_paradise_initiative_tooltip
		}
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_ecology days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					has_global_flag = ecology_pops_patch_flag
					OR = {
						has_policy_flag = eco_policy_environmental_selfregulation
						has_policy_flag = eco_policy_environmental_exploitation
						has_policy_flag = eco_policy_environmental_deregulation
						has_policy_flag = eco_environmental_policy_default
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = diploevent.3 }
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_ecology days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_ecology_environmental_control_board"
	}
	
	breach = {
		has_global_flag = ecology_pops_patch_flag
		has_policy_flag = eco_environmental_policy_default
	}

	ai_weight = {

			factor = 0.9
			is_civic_expansionist = yes

		}
		
		modifier = {

				NOT = {
					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }
				}
				in_breach_of = resolution_ecology_paradise_initiative
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 5

		}

			factor = 2
			OR = {
				is_civic_has_meritocracy = yes
				is_civic_machine_servitor = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_egalitarian = yes
			OR = {
				has_technology = tech_selected_lineages
				has_technology = tech_capacity_boosters
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_beacon_of_liberty
				has_valid_civic = civic_idealistic_foundation
			}
			OR = {
				has_technology = tech_selected_lineages
				has_technology = tech_capacity_boosters
			}
		}

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_federation_ally = {
				NOT = {
					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }
				}
				in_breach_of = resolution_galacticstudies_ethical_guideline_refactoring
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {

			}

		custom_tooltip = resolution_galacticstudies_advanced_xenostudies_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_galacticstudies days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_xenophile_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					OR = {
						AND = {
							can_set_ai_policy = yes
							has_policy_flag = ai_outlawed
						}

						AND = {
							has_met_primitives = yes
							has_policy_flag = interference_passive
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = federations.10100 }
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_galacticstudies days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_galacticstudies_astral_studies_network"
	}

	breach = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				can_set_ai_policy = yes
				has_policy_flag = ai_outlawed
			}

			AND = {
				has_met_primitives = yes
				has_policy_flag = interference_passive
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			count_country = {
				count < 4
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					relative_power = { who = prev category = technology value >= equivalent }
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			any_relation = {
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_rival = prev
					is_at_war_with = prev
				}
				count_country = {
					count < 4
					limit = {
						is_galactic_community_member = yes
						relative_power = { who = prev category = technology value >= equivalent }
					}
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_materialist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_materialist = yes
			is_xenophile = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_merchant_guilds
				has_valid_civic = civic_philosopher_king
			}
			is_xenophile = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_xenophile = no
			is_spiritualist = no
			any_planet_within_border = {
				has_observation_outpost = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_xenophobe = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_system_within_border = {
				any_fleet_in_system = {
					exists = owner
					owner = { is_country_type = enclave }
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_spiritualist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_xenophile = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
			is_materialist = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = robot_exploiter
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = robot_liberator
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			in_breach_of = resolution_galacticstudies_advanced_xenostudies
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			any_federation_ally = {
				NOT = {
					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }
				}
				in_breach_of = resolution_galacticstudies_advanced_xenostudies
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_spiritualist = no
			is_xenophile = no

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			any_federation_ally = {
				NOT = {
					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }
				}
				in_breach_of = resolution_galacticstudies_ethical_guideline_refactoring
			}
		}
		modifier = {

			NOT = { in_breach_of = resolution_galacticstudies_ethical_guideline_refactoring }
			any_relation = {
				is_galactic_community_member = yes

		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 1

	modifier = {
		resolution_commerce_buzzword_standardization = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_commerce days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_commerce days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOR = {
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_commerce_buzzword_standardization"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_commerce_leveraged_privateering"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_commerce_underdeveloped_system_utilization"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_commerce_holistic_asset_coordination"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_commerce_profit_maximization_engines"
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_loved
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			count_country = {
				count < 4
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					relative_power = { who = prev category = economy value >= equivalent }
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			any_relation = {
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_rival = prev
					is_at_war_with = prev
				}
				count_country = {
					count < 4
					limit = {
						is_galactic_community_member = yes
						relative_power = { who = prev category = economy value >= equivalent }
					}
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_auth_corporate = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			is_civic_free_traders = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_anti_corp = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_valid_civic = civic_byzantine_bureaucracy
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_civic_efficient_bureaucracy = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_civic_shared_burden = yes
			is_auth_corporate = no
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_valid_civic = civic_barbaric_despoilers
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			is_gestalt = yes
		}
	}
}

			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_commerce days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_commerce_buzzword_standardization"
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_militarist = no
			count_country = {
				count < 4
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					relative_power = { who = prev category = economy value >= equivalent }
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			any_relation = {
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_rival = prev
					is_at_war_with = prev
				}
				count_country = {
					count < 4
					limit = {
						is_galactic_community_member = yes
						relative_power = { who = prev category = economy value >= equivalent }
					}
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_auth_corporate = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			is_auth_corporate = no
			is_gestalt = no
			NOT = {
				any_system_within_border = {
					trade_intercepted_percentage >= 20
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_gestalt = no
			any_system_within_border = {
				trade_intercepted_percentage >= 40
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_gestalt = no
			any_system_within_border = {
				trade_intercepted_percentage >= 60
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_gestalt = no
			any_system_within_border = {
				trade_intercepted_percentage >= 80
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_anti_corp = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_valid_civic = civic_byzantine_bureaucracy
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_militarist = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_civic_militarist = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_civic_shared_burden = yes
			is_auth_corporate = no
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			is_militarist = no
			is_anti_corp = no
			any_system_within_border = {
				has_trade_route = yes
				trade_intercepted_value >= 30
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_owned_planet = {
				planet_crime > 40
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_criminal_syndicate = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.1
			is_gestalt = yes
		}
	}
}

		hidden_effect = {
			pass_resolution = "resolution_industry_collective_waste_management"
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_industry_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_industry_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_industry_building_a_better_tomorrow"
	}

		resolution_industry_regulatory_facilitation = 1
		resolution_industry_collective_waste_management = 1
	}

	allow = {}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_unpopular
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.9
			is_civic_expansionist = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			count_country = {
				count < 4
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					relative_power = { who = prev category = economy value >= equivalent }
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_relation = {
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_rival = prev
					is_at_war_with = prev
				}
				count_country = {
					count < 4
					limit = {
						is_galactic_community_member = yes
						relative_power = { who = prev category = economy value >= equivalent }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_valid_civic = civic_starvation_fearing
			is_lithoid_empire = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
		}
		
		modifier = {

		}

			is_militarist = yes
		}
		modifier = {

			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
		}

		}

			owner_species = { has_trait = eco_trait_clean }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			owner_species = { has_trait = eco_trait_dirty }

		}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			is_civic_expansionist = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			count_country = {
				count < 4
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					relative_power = { who = prev category = economy value >= equivalent }
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			any_relation = {
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_rival = prev
					is_at_war_with = prev
				}
				count_country = {
					count < 4
					limit = {
						is_galactic_community_member = yes
						relative_power = { who = prev category = economy value >= equivalent }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_valid_civic = civic_starvation_fearing
			is_lithoid_empire = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_militarist = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_civic_militarist = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_civic_has_elite = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_slaver = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				is_civic_environmentalist = yes
				AND = {
					has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
					is_lithoid_empire = no
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			owner_species = { has_trait = eco_trait_clean }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			owner_species = { has_trait = eco_trait_dirty }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_civic_functional_architecture = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_valid_civic = civic_agribusiness
			is_lithoid_empire = no
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			owner_species = {
				OR = {
					has_trait = trait_nonadaptive
					has_trait = trait_endemic
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_monthly_income = { resource = minerals  value < 50 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_monthly_income = { resource = alloys  value < 25 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_deficit = minerals
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_deficit = alloys
		}
	}
}

resolution_greatergood_repeal_1 = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_council_veto"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_greatergood_repeal_1_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_greatergood_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_egalitarian_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_greatergood_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_workers_rights"
	}

	allow = {}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_unpopular

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_civic_machine_servitor = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_authoritarian = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_has_elite = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_civic_has_meritocracy = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
				is_civic_free_haven = yes
				is_civic_inwards_perfection = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			OR = {
				is_civic_slaver_guilds = yes
				is_origin_syncretic_livestock = yes
				is_slaver = yes
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = slaver
			}
		}
	}
}

resolution_greatergood_repeal_2 = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_council_veto"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t2
		}
	}
	target = no

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_greatergood_repeal_2_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			pass_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_workers_rights"
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_greatergood_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_egalitarian_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
			if = {
				limit = { is_authoritarian = no }
				set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_xenophile_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_greatergood_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans"
	}

	modifier = {
		resolution_greatergood_workers_rights = 1
	}

	allow = {}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_unpopular

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			NOT = { in_breach_of = resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans }
			is_xenophile = yes
			is_authoritarian = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			NOT = { in_breach_of = resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans }
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
			is_authoritarian = no
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_civic_machine_servitor = yes
		}

				modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_authoritarian = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_has_elite = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_civic_has_meritocracy = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			in_breach_of = resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_federation_ally = {
				NOT = {
					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }
				}
				in_breach_of = resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
				is_civic_free_haven = yes
				is_civic_inwards_perfection = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			OR = {
				is_civic_slaver_guilds = yes
				is_origin_syncretic_livestock = yes
				is_slaver = yes
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = slaver
			}
		}
	}
}

			is_authoritarian = no

				free_housing < 1
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75

					is_rival = prev

resolution_greatergood_workers_rights = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_greater_good"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 1

	modifier = {
		resolution_greatergood_workers_rights = 1
	}
	
	breach = {
		AND = {
			has_global_flag = expanded_pops_active
			has_policy_flag = no_union_rights
		}
	}

	effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = expanded_pops_active }
			custom_tooltip = resolution_greatergood_workers_rights_tooltip
			hidden_effect = {
				set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
				every_playable_country = {
					limit = {
						is_galactic_community_member = yes
						is_gestalt = no
						has_policy_flag = no_union_rights
					}
					country_event = { id = diploevent.4 }
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_civic_slaver_guilds = yes
						is_origin_syncretic_livestock = yes
						is_slaver = yes
					}
				}
				set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_authoritarian_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOR = {
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_workers_rights"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_balance_in_the_middle"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_universal_prosperity_mandate"
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_loved

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_civic_has_elite = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_civic_has_meritocracy = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ai_personality_behaviour = slaver
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_auth_corporate = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			OR = {
				is_civic_shared_burden = yes
				is_civic_machine_servitor = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
				is_civic_free_haven = yes
				is_civic_inwards_perfection = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_gestalt = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_civic_authoritarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				is_civic_slaver_guilds = yes
				is_origin_syncretic_livestock = yes
				is_slaver = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

	icon = "GFX_resolution_greater_good"

		}
	}

	level = 2

	}

		custom_tooltip = resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						is_civic_slaver_guilds = yes

resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_greater_good"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t3
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 3

	modifier = {
		resolution_greatergood_workers_rights = 1
		resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans = 1
		resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves_tooltip

		hidden_effect = {
			every_playable_country = {
				limit = { is_galactic_community_member = yes }
				country_event = { id = federations.10010 days = 15 }
			}

			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes

					OR = {
						any_enslaved_species = {
							is_sapient = yes
							OR = {
								has_slavery_type = { type = slavery_normal country = prev  }
								has_slavery_type = { type = slavery_livestock country = prev }
								has_slavery_type = { type = slavery_matrix country = prev }
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_gestalt = no
							any_owned_species = {
								is_sapient = yes
								OR = {
									has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
									has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_stratified country = prev }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = federations.10210 }
			}

			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_authoritarian_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans"
	}

	breach = {
		OR = {
			any_enslaved_species = {
				is_sapient = yes
				OR = {
					has_slavery_type = { type = slavery_normal country = prev }
					has_slavery_type = { type = slavery_livestock country = prev }
					has_slavery_type = { type = slavery_matrix country = prev }
				}
			}
			AND = {
				is_gestalt = no
				any_owned_species = {
					is_sapient = yes
					OR = {
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_stratified country = prev }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = { in_breach_of = resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves }
			is_xenophile = yes
			is_authoritarian = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { in_breach_of = resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves }
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
			is_authoritarian = no
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_civic_authoritarian = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_civic_has_elite = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_civic_has_meritocracy = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			in_breach_of = resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			any_federation_ally = {
				NOT = {
					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }
				}
				in_breach_of = resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_auth_corporate = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			OR = {
				is_civic_shared_burden = yes
				is_civic_machine_servitor = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			OR = {
				is_gestalt = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				is_civic_slaver_guilds = yes
				is_origin_syncretic_livestock = yes
				is_slaver = yes
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = slaver
				any_owned_species = {
					is_sapient = yes
					OR = {
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_stratified country = prev }
					}
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
				is_civic_free_haven = yes
				is_civic_inwards_perfection = yes

resolution_greatergood_balance_in_the_middle = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_greater_good"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t4
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 4

	modifier = {
		resolution_greatergood_workers_rights = 1
		resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans = 1
		resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves = 1
		resolution_greatergood_balance_in_the_middle = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_greatergood_balance_in_the_middle_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_authoritarian_outraged_gc days = 7200 }

			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes

					OR = {
						any_owned_species = {
							is_sapient = yes
							has_citizenship_type = { type = citizenship_slavery country = prev }
						}
						AND = {
							is_gestalt = no
							any_owned_species = {
								is_sapient = yes
								OR = {
									has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
									has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_stratified country = prev }
									has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_normal country = prev }
									has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_academic_privilege country = prev }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = federations.10220 }
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves"
	}

	breach = {
		OR = {
			is_civic_slaver_guilds = yes
			any_owned_species = {
				is_sapient = yes
				has_citizenship_type = { type = citizenship_slavery country = prev }
			}
			AND = {
				is_gestalt = no
				any_owned_species = {
					is_sapient = yes
					OR = {
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_stratified country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_normal country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_academic_privilege country = prev }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_unpopular

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_xenophile = yes
			is_authoritarian = no
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
			is_authoritarian = no
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				is_authoritarian = yes
				is_civic_authoritarian = yes
				is_civic_has_elite = yes
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_has_meritocracy = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			in_breach_of = resolution_greatergood_balance_in_the_middle
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			any_federation_ally = {
				NOT = {
					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }
				}
				in_breach_of = resolution_greatergood_balance_in_the_middle
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_auth_corporate = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			OR = {
				is_civic_shared_burden = yes
				is_civic_machine_servitor = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.6
			OR = {
				is_gestalt = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				is_civic_slaver_guilds = yes
				is_origin_syncretic_livestock = yes
				is_slaver = yes
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = slaver
				any_owned_species = {
					is_sapient = yes
					OR = {
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_stratified country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_normal country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_academic_privilege country = prev }
					}
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_agrarian_idyll
				is_civic_free_haven = yes
				is_civic_inwards_perfection = yes
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			any_owned_planet = {
				free_housing < 1
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_authoritarian = no
			is_gestalt = no
			NOT = { in_breach_of = resolution_greatergood_balance_in_the_middle }
			any_relation = {
				OR = {
					is_rival = prev
					is_at_war_with = prev
				}
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				in_breach_of = resolution_greatergood_balance_in_the_middle
			}
		}
	}
}

resolution_greatergood_universal_prosperity_mandate = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_greater_good"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t5
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 5

	modifier = {
		resolution_greatergood_workers_rights = 1
		resolution_greatergood_five_year_plans = 1
		resolution_greatergood_greater_than_ourselves = 1
		resolution_greatergood_balance_in_the_middle = 1
		resolution_greatergood_universal_prosperity_mandate = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_greatergood_universal_prosperity_mandate_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_greatergood days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_authoritarian_outraged_gc days = 7200 }

			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes

					OR = {
						any_owned_species = {
							is_sapient = yes
							has_citizenship_type = { type = citizenship_slavery country = prev }
						}
						AND = {
							is_gestalt = no
							any_owned_species = {
								is_sapient = yes
								OR = {
									has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
									has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_stratified country = prev }
									has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_normal country = prev }
									has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_academic_privilege country = prev }
									has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_good country = prev }
								}
							}
						}
						AND = {
							is_gestalt = yes
							any_owned_species = {
								is_sapient = yes
								OR = {
									has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_ego_assimilation country = prev }
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}

		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_greatergood_balance_in_the_middle"
	}

	breach = {
		OR = {
			is_civic_slaver_guilds = yes
			AND = {
				is_gestalt = no
				any_owned_species = {
					is_sapient = yes
					OR = {
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_stratified country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_normal country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_academic_privilege country = prev }
						has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_good country = prev }
					}
				}
			}
			any_owned_species = {
				is_sapient = yes
				has_citizenship_type = { type = citizenship_slavery country = prev }
			}
			AND = {

					OR = {

resolution_mutualdefense_repeal_1 = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_red"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_mutualdefense_repeal_1_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_mutualdefense_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_militarist_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_mutualdefense_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_the_readied_shield"
	}

	allow = {}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_unpopular
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			count_country = {
				count < 4
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					relative_power = { who = prev category = fleet value >= equivalent }
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_relation = {
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_rival = prev
					is_at_war_with = prev
				}
				count_country = {
					count < 4
					limit = {
						is_galactic_community_member = yes
						relative_power = { who = prev category = fleet value >= equivalent }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			OR = {
				is_at_war = yes
				has_crisis = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				is_militarist = yes
				is_civic_militarist = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_pacifist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_pacifist
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			is_civic_inwards_perfection = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_xenophobic_isolationists = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_diplomatic_corps = yes
		}
	}
}

				has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				is_in_breach_of_any = yes
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			in_breach_of = resolution_mutualdefense_military_readiness_act
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			used_naval_capacity_percent < 0.25
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			used_naval_capacity_percent < 0.1
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			OR = {
				is_at_war = yes
				has_crisis = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				is_militarist = yes
				is_civic_militarist = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_pacifist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_pacifist
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			is_civic_inwards_perfection = yes
		}
		modifier = {

			is_xenophobic_isolationists = yes

					is_at_war_with = prev

					is_galactic_community_member = no

		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOR = {
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_the_readied_shield"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_military_readiness_act"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_enemy_of_my_enemy"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_castigation_proclamation"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_renegade_containment"
			}
		}

			count_country = {
				count < 4
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					relative_power = { who = prev category = fleet value >= equivalent }
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			any_relation = {
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_rival = prev
					is_at_war_with = prev
				}
				count_country = {
					count < 4
					limit = {
						is_galactic_community_member = yes
						relative_power = { who = prev category = fleet value >= equivalent }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			OR = {
				is_at_war = yes
				has_crisis = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_militarist = yes

				is_civic_diplomatic_corps = yes
				is_civic_free_traders = yes
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			used_naval_capacity_percent < 0.5
			is_militarist = no
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5

		}

resolution_mutualdefense_castigation_denouncement = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_mutual_defense"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_denounce
		}
	}

	target = yes
	harmful = yes
	valid_target = {
		OR = {
			is_country_type = default
			is_country_type = ascended_empire
			is_country_type = lost_empire
		}
		NOT = { is_same_value = from } # don't denounce yourself.
		OR = {
			is_galactic_community_member = no
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
		}
		OR = {
			opinion_level = { who = from level < neutral }
			from = { is_rival = prev }
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
		}
		OR = {
			is_galactic_emperor = no
			imperial_authority <= 100
		}
	}

	effect = {
		add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_denounced days = 3600 }
	}

	potential = {
		OR = {
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_castigation_proclamation"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_renegade_containment"
		}
	}

	allow = {
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			FROM = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
			imperial_authority >= 75
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			FROM = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
			imperial_authority >= 50
		}
		# Never on yourself
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_same_value = from
		}
		# More likely against rival
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_rival = from
		}
	}
}

resolution_council_denouncement = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_purges"

	potential = {
		OR = {
			has_federations_dlc = yes
			has_nemesis = yes
		}
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}

	target = yes
	harmful = yes
	valid_target = {
		OR = {
			is_country_type = default
			is_country_type = ascended_empire
			is_country_type = lost_empire
		}
		is_galactic_community_member = yes
		NOT = { is_same_value = from } # don't denounce yourself.
		OR = {
			opinion_level = { who = from level < neutral }
			from = { is_rival = prev }
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
		}
		OR = {
			is_galactic_emperor = no
			imperial_authority <= 100
		}
	}

	effect = {
		add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_denounced days = 3600 }
	}

	potential = {
		is_galactic_council_established = yes
		NOT = { has_global_flag = resolution_council_denouncement_abolished }
	}

	allow = {
		is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_disliked
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			FROM = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
			imperial_authority >= 75
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			FROM = { is_galactic_emperor = yes }
			imperial_authority >= 50
		}
		# Never on yourself
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_same_value = from
		}
		# More likely against rival
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_rival = from
		}
		
		# weaklings are scared of BtC
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			has_nemesis = yes
			any_playable_country = {
				#has_crisis_level >= crisis_level_1
				OR = {
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_1
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_2
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_3
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_4
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_5
				}
				NOT = { is_same_value = prev }
				has_resource = {
					type = menace
					amount > 1000
				}
				relative_power = {
					who = prev
					category = all
					value > equivalent
				}
			}
		}

		# everyone is scared of BtC
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			has_nemesis = yes
			any_playable_country = {
				#has_crisis_level >= crisis_level_1
				OR = {
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_1
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_2
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_3
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_4
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_5
				}
				NOT = { is_same_value = prev }
				has_resource = {
					type = menace
					amount > 2000
				}
			}
		}

		# imagine having a BtC empire next door
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			has_nemesis = yes
			any_neighbor_country = {
				#has_crisis_level >= crisis_level_1
				OR = {
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_1
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_2
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_3
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_4
					has_crisis_level = crisis_level_5
				}
			}
		}

		# imagine your rival having a (not too scary) BtC empire next door - that's good
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.01
			has_nemesis = yes
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					#has_crisis_level >= crisis_level_1
					OR = {
						has_crisis_level = crisis_level_1
						has_crisis_level = crisis_level_2
						has_crisis_level = crisis_level_3
						has_crisis_level = crisis_level_4
						has_crisis_level = crisis_level_5
					}
				}
			}
			any_rival_country = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					#has_crisis_level >= crisis_level_1
					#has_crisis_level < crisis_level_5
					OR = {
						has_crisis_level = crisis_level_1
						has_crisis_level = crisis_level_2
						has_crisis_level = crisis_level_3
						has_crisis_level = crisis_level_4
						#has_crisis_level = crisis_level_5
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}


# RULES OF WAR

resolution_rulesofwar_repeal_1 = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_red"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_rulesofwar_repeal_1_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_rulesofwar_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_pacifist_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_xenophobe_isolationist_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_rulesofwar_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_rulesofwar_guardian_angels"
	}

	allow = {}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_unpopular	
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			count_country = {
				count < 4
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					relative_power = { who = prev category = fleet value >= equivalent }
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			any_relation = {
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_rival = prev
					is_at_war_with = prev
				}
				count_country = {
					count < 4
					limit = {
						is_galactic_community_member = yes
						relative_power = { who = prev category = fleet value >= equivalent }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_militarist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_militarist = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_ai_personality = vb_keepers_of_peace
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				is_open_gestalt = yes
				is_civic_machine_servitor = yes
				is_civic_diplomatic_corps = yes
				is_civic_inwards_perfection = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_pacifist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_xenophobic_isolationists = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_ascension_perk = ap_become_the_crisis
		}
	}
}

resolution_rulesofwar_repeal_2 = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_red"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t2
		}
	}
	target = no

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_rulesofwar_repeal_2_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			pass_resolution = "resolution_rulesofwar_guardian_angels"
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_rulesofwar_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_pacifist_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_xenophobe_isolationist_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_protect_neutrals" }
			custom_tooltip = resolution_repeal_protect_neutrals_tooltip
			hidden_effect = {
				pass_resolution = resolution_repeal_protect_neutrals
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_rulesofwar_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life"
	}

	modifier = {
		resolution_rulesofwar_guardian_angels = 1
	}

	allow = {}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_unpopular
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			count_country = {
				count < 4
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					relative_power = { who = prev category = fleet value >= equivalent }
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			any_relation = {
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_rival = prev
					is_at_war_with = prev
				}
				count_country = {
					count < 4
					limit = {
						is_galactic_community_member = yes
						relative_power = { who = prev category = fleet value >= equivalent }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { in_breach_of = resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life }
			any_relation = {
				OR = {
					is_rival = prev
					is_at_war_with = prev
				}
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				in_breach_of = resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 100
			OR = { has_civic = civic_living_hosts has_origin = origin_necrophage }
			is_pacifist = no
			is_xenophobic_isolationists = no
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_militarist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_militarist = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			in_breach_of = resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_federation_ally = {
				NOT = {
					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }
				}
				in_breach_of = resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_ai_personality = vb_keepers_of_peace
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				is_open_gestalt = yes
				is_civic_machine_servitor = yes
				is_civic_diplomatic_corps = yes
				is_civic_inwards_perfection = yes
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_xenophile = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_pacifist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_xenophobic_isolationists = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_ascension_perk = ap_become_the_crisis
		}
	}
}

		}

			factor = 2

		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_militarist = yes
			NOT = { has_ai_personality = vb_keepers_of_peace }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_ai_personality_behaviour = conqueror
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			in_breach_of = resolution_rulesofwar_last_resort_doctrine
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_federation_ally = {
				NOT = {
					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }
				}
				in_breach_of = resolution_rulesofwar_last_resort_doctrine
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			has_ai_personality = vb_keepers_of_peace
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				is_open_gestalt = yes
				is_civic_machine_servitor = yes
				is_civic_diplomatic_corps = yes
				is_civic_inwards_perfection = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_pacifist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_xenophobic_isolationists = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_ascension_perk = ap_become_the_crisis
		}
	}
}

		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_rulesofwar_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_rulesofwar_demobilization_initiative"
	}

	modifier = {
		resolution_rulesofwar_guardian_angels = 1
		resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life = 1
		resolution_rulesofwar_independent_tribunals = 1
		resolution_rulesofwar_last_resort_doctrine = 1
	}

	allow = {}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_unpopular
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			count_country = {
				count < 4
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					relative_power = { who = prev category = fleet value >= equivalent }
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			any_relation = {
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_rival = prev
					is_at_war_with = prev
				}
				count_country = {
					count < 4
					limit = {
						is_galactic_community_member = yes
						relative_power = { who = prev category = fleet value >= equivalent }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			NOT = { in_breach_of = resolution_rulesofwar_demobilization_initiative }
			any_relation = {
				OR = {
					is_rival = prev
					is_at_war_with = prev
				}
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				in_breach_of = resolution_rulesofwar_demobilization_initiative
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			is_pacifist = no
			is_xenophobic_isolationists = no
			has_ascension_perk = ap_colossus
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 100
			OR = { has_civic = civic_living_hosts has_origin = origin_necrophage }
			is_pacifist = no
			is_xenophobic_isolationists = no
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_militarist = yes
			NOT = { has_ai_personality = vb_keepers_of_peace }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
			NOT = { has_ai_personality = vb_keepers_of_peace }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_militarist = yes
			NOT = { has_ai_personality = vb_keepers_of_peace }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			in_breach_of = resolution_rulesofwar_demobilization_initiative
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_federation_ally = {
				NOT = {
					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }
				}
				in_breach_of = resolution_rulesofwar_demobilization_initiative
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ai_personality = vb_keepers_of_peace
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				is_open_gestalt = yes
				is_civic_machine_servitor = yes
				is_civic_diplomatic_corps = yes
				is_civic_inwards_perfection = yes
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				is_at_war = yes
				has_crisis = yes
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			in_breach_of = resolution_mutualdefense_military_readiness_act
			OR = {
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_military_readiness_act"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_enemy_of_my_enemy"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_castigation_proclamation"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_mutualdefense_renegade_containment"
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_pacifist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_xenophobic_isolationists = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_ascension_perk = ap_become_the_crisis
		}
	}
}

resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_rules_of_war"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t2
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 2

	modifier = {
		resolution_rulesofwar_guardian_angels = 1
		resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_rulesofwar days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_ai_personality = vb_keepers_of_peace } }
				set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_militarist_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_ai_personality_behaviour = purger
						AND = {
							has_origin = origin_necrophage
							is_pacifist = no
							is_xenophobic_isolationists = no
						}
					}
				}
				set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_xenophobe_supremacist_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
			}

			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					has_policy_flag = purge_allowed
				}
				country_event = { id = federations.10300 }
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_rulesofwar days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_rulesofwar_guardian_angels"
	}

	breach = {
		OR = {
			has_policy_flag = purge_allowed
			has_country_flag = resolution_breached_fired_cracker
		}
	}

		weight = @resolution_weight_popular

			factor = 0.5
			count_country = {
				count < 4
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					relative_power = { who = prev category = fleet value >= equivalent }
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_relation = {
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_rival = prev
					is_at_war_with = prev
				}
				count_country = {
					count < 4
					limit = {
						is_galactic_community_member = yes
						relative_power = { who = prev category = fleet value >= equivalent }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOT = { in_breach_of = resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life }
			any_relation = {
				OR = {
					is_rival = prev
					is_at_war_with = prev
				}
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				in_breach_of = resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life
			}

			is_xenophobic_isolationists = no

		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0

		}

		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0

		resolution_rulesofwar_reverence_for_life = 1
		resolution_rulesofwar_independent_tribunals = 1
		resolution_rulesofwar_last_resort_doctrine = 1
		resolution_rulesofwar_demobilization_initiative = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_rulesofwar_demobilization_initiative_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_rulesofwar days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_ai_personality = vb_keepers_of_peace } }
				set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_militarist_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
			}
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_xenophobe_supremacist_outraged_gc days = 7200 }

			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					has_policy_flag = economic_policy_military
				}
				country_event = { id = federations.10330 }
			}
		}
	}

resolution_divinity_a_defined_purpose = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_robots_bad"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t5
		}
	}
	target = no
	level = 5

	modifier = {
		resolution_divinity_comfort_the_fallen = 1
		resolution_divinity_tithe_on_the_soulless = 1
		resolution_divinity_right_to_work = 1
		resolution_divinity_silence_the_soulless = 1
		resolution_divinity_a_defined_purpose = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_divinity_a_defined_purpose_effect
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_divinity days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_materialist_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
			every_playable_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					in_breach_of = resolution_divinity_a_defined_purpose
				}
				country_event = { id = federations.10340 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_global_flag = resolution_ascension_cyborg_flag }
			custom_tooltip = resolution_repeal_ascension_cyborg_effect_success
			hidden_effect = {
				remove_global_flag = resolution_ascension_cyborg_flag
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_divinity days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_divinity_silence_the_soulless"
	}

	breach = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				is_synthetic_empire = no
				has_policy_flag = ai_full_rights
			}
			AND = {
				is_machine_empire = yes
				NOT = { has_country_flag = synthetic_empire }
				NOT = { has_civic = civic_machine_servitor }
			}
			AND = {
				has_country_flag = synthetic_empire
				OR = {
					any_owned_species = {
						is_sapient = yes
						is_robotic = no
						OR = {
							has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_subsistence country = prev }
							has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_stratified country = prev }
							has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_normal country = prev }
							has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_academic_privilege country = prev }
							has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_good country = prev }
						}
					}
					any_owned_species = {
						is_sapient = yes
						is_robotic = no
						has_citizenship_type = { type = citizenship_slavery country = prev }
					}
				}
			}
			any_owned_species = {
				is_sapient = yes
				OR = {
					has_living_standard = { type = living_standard_tech_assimilation country = prev }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_disliked
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			count_country = {
				count < 4
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					relative_power = { who = prev category = technology value >= equivalent }
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_machine_empire = no
			is_civic_materialist = no
			any_relation = {
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_rival = prev
					is_at_war_with = prev
				}
				count_country = {
					count < 4
					limit = {
						is_galactic_community_member = yes
						relative_power = { who = prev category = technology value >= equivalent }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			NOR = {
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = robot_exploiter
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = robot_liberator
			}
			is_materialist = no
			is_spiritualist = no
			any_relation = {
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_rival = prev
					is_at_war_with = prev
				}
				OR = {
					has_ai_personality_behaviour = robot_exploiter
					has_ai_personality_behaviour = robot_liberator
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOR = {
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = robot_exploiter
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = robot_liberator
			}
			is_materialist = no
			is_spiritualist = yes
			any_relation = {
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_rival = prev
					is_at_war_with = prev
				}
				OR = {
					has_ai_personality_behaviour = robot_exploiter
					has_ai_personality_behaviour = robot_liberator
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5

		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			has_ai_personality_behaviour = robot_liberator
			NOT = { has_civic = civic_machine_servitor }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_gestalt = yes
			NOT = { has_civic = civic_machine_servitor }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_synthetic_empire = yes
			NOT = { has_civic = civic_machine_servitor }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			any_federation_ally = {
				NOT = {
					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }
				}
				is_synthetic_empire = yes
				NOT = { has_civic = civic_machine_servitor }
			}

		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_spiritualist = yes
		}

			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_authoritarian_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_hated

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			is_democratic_crusaders = no
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_part_of_galactic_council = no
			has_ai_personality = democratic_crusaders
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_part_of_galactic_council = no
			has_ai_personality = egalitarian_imperialists
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_subject = yes
			overlord = {
				opinion_level = { who = prev level >= neutral }
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				is_civic_diplomatic_corps = yes
				is_civic_machine_servitor = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.33
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.33
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				is_gestalt = yes
				is_xenophobe = yes
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_xenophile = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}
		modifier = {

			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
		}
	}

resolution_galacticreforms_form_council = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_create_council"

	potential = {
		OR = {
			has_federations_dlc = yes
			has_nemesis = yes
		}
		NOT = { has_global_flag = galactic_council_formed }
		has_galactic_emperor = no
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no

	modifier = {
	}

	allow = {
		is_years_since_community_formation >= 20
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_galacticreforms_form_council_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_council_size = 3
			set_council_veto = no
			remove_global_flag = resolution_council_denouncement_abolished
			set_global_flag = galactic_council_formed
			set_global_flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed

			set_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed # council denouncement

			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_xenophobe_isolationist_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_loved

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			galactic_community_rank <= 3
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				is_authoritarian = yes
				has_ai_personality_behaviour = subjugator
			}
			galactic_community_rank <= 3
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				is_civic_diplomatic_corps = yes
				is_civic_machine_servitor = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.75
			OR = {
				galactic_community_rank <= 3
				AND = {
					is_subject = yes
					overlord = {
						opinion_level = { who = prev level >= neutral }
						galactic_community_rank <= 3
					}
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			OR = {
				is_gestalt = yes
				is_xenophobe = yes
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_xenophobic_isolationists = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			galactic_community_rank > 5
			NAND = {
				is_subject = yes
				overlord = {
					opinion_level = { who = prev level >= neutral }
					galactic_community_rank <= 3
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {

			}

			}

		}
		modifier = {
