	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t3
		}
	}
	target = no

	modifier = {
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		set_council_size = 5
		set_global_flag = galactic_council_formed

		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_popular

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			num_council_positions = 4
			OR = {
				galactic_community_rank = 5
				AND = {
					is_subject = yes
					overlord = {
						opinion_level = { who = prev level >= neutral }
						galactic_community_rank = 5
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			num_council_positions = 4
			galactic_community_rank = 5
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
			is_egalitarian = no
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_civic_diplomatic_corps = yes
		}
	}
}

resolution_galacticreforms_permanent_seat = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_council_member_permanent"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
		is_galactic_council_established = yes
		has_galactic_emperor = no
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t5
		}
	}

	target = yes
	harmful = no
	valid_target = {
		OR = {
			is_country_type = default
			is_country_type = ascended_empire
			is_country_type = lost_empire
		}
		is_galactic_community_member = yes
		is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
		is_permanent_councillor = no
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		add_permanent_councillor = yes
	}

	potential = {
		is_galactic_council_established = yes
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_disliked
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_part_of_galactic_council = no
			is_egalitarian = yes
			NOT = { is_same_value = from }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_part_of_galactic_council = no
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
			NOT = { is_same_value = from }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
		}
		# More likely to vote for yourself
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			is_same_value = from
			NOT = { has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			is_same_value = from
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
		}
		# Never vote for your rival
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_rival = from
		}
	}
}

resolution_sanctions_tech_repeal_1 = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_blue"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_denounce
		}
	}
	target = no

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = resolution_sanctions_tech_repeal_1_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_sanctions_tech_1"
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_unpopular

		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_in_breach_of_any = no
			is_materialist = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.25
			is_in_breach_of_any = no
			is_civic_materialist = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_relation = {
				is_in_federation_with = prev
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			any_relation = {
				is_rival = prev
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

resolution_sanctions_tech_1 = {
	icon = "GFX_sanctions_blue"
	level = 1

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_denounce
		}
	}

	target = no

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = sanctions_effect
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
			set_timed_global_flag = { flag = recent_galcom_sanctions_passed years = 10 }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	modifier = {
	}

	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			OR = {
				is_in_breach_of_any = yes
				has_modifier = resolution_denounced
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			resolution_sanctions_tech = 1
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "requires_something_illegal"
			has_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOR = {
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_sanctions_tech_1"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_sanctions_tech_2"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_sanctions_tech_3"
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			has_global_flag = recent_galcom_sanctions_passed
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_in_breach_of_any = no
			is_materialist = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_in_breach_of_any = no
			is_civic_materialist = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			any_relation = {
				is_in_federation_with = prev
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			any_relation = {
				is_rival = prev
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		}
		
		modifier = {

resolution_sanctions_military_1 = {
	icon = "GFX_sanctions_red"
	level = 1

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_denounce
		}
	}

	target = no

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = sanctions_effect
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
			set_timed_global_flag = { flag = recent_galcom_sanctions_passed years = 10 }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	modifier = {
	}

	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			OR = {
				is_in_breach_of_any = yes
				has_modifier = resolution_denounced
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			resolution_sanctions_military = 1
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "requires_something_illegal"
			has_global_flag = resolution_with_breach_effect_passed
		}
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOR = {
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_sanctions_military_1"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_sanctions_military_2"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_sanctions_military_3"
			}
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			has_global_flag = recent_galcom_sanctions_passed
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_in_breach_of_any = no
			OR = {
				is_militarist = yes
				is_pacifist = yes
				is_xenophobic_isolationists = yes
				is_open_gestalt = yes
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_in_breach_of_any = no
			is_civic_militarist = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			any_relation = {
				is_in_federation_with = prev
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			any_relation = {
				is_rival = prev
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

resolution_sanctions_administrative_2 = {
	icon = "GFX_sanctions_purple"
	level = 2

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_denounce
		}
	}

	target = no

	effect = {
		custom_tooltip = sanctions_effect
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
			set_timed_global_flag = { flag = recent_galcom_sanctions_passed years = 10 }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	modifier = {
	}

	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			OR = {
				is_in_breach_of_any = yes
				has_modifier = resolution_denounced
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			resolution_sanctions_administrative = 2
		}
	}

	allow = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_sanctions_administrative_1"
		is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_in_breach_of_any = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.33
			has_global_flag = recent_galcom_sanctions_passed
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			is_in_breach_of_any = no
			OR = {
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				is_xenophile = yes
				is_civic_diplomatic_corps = yes
				is_civic_machine_servitor = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			any_relation = {
				is_in_federation_with = prev
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			any_relation = {
				is_rival = prev
				is_galactic_community_member = yes
				OR = {
					is_in_breach_of_any = yes
					has_modifier = resolution_denounced
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# GALACTIC FOCUS RESOLUTIONS

resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_prethoryn = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_emergency_measure"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no

	modifier = {
		resolution_end_game = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_prethoryn_effect_success

		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_prethoryn
			set_global_flag = galactic_community_crisis_fighting

			remove_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_unbidden
			remove_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_contingency
			remove_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_greatkhan
			remove_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_nanites

			set_global_flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_global_flag = ongoing_prethoryn_invasion
		NOT = { has_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_prethoryn }
	}

	allow = {
	}

	active = { # Resolution only in effect while this trigger is met
		has_global_flag = ongoing_prethoryn_invasion
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_normal
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_modifier = prepared_for_the_end
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			any_neighbor_country = {
				is_country_type = swarm
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			any_relation = {
				is_in_federation_with = prev
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_country_type = swarm
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_relation = {
				has_defensive_pact = prev
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_country_type = swarm
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			any_relation = {
				is_rival = prev
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_country_type = swarm
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_country_type = swarm
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75

			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_country_type = swarm
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75

			has_crisis_stage_1 = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2

			has_crisis_stage_3 = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 15

			has_crisis_stage_4 = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 50

			has_ascension_perk = ap_defender_of_the_galaxy
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_philosopher_king
				is_civic_diplomatic_corps = yes
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
				is_civic_inwards_perfection = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			is_militarist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			is_xenophile = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_pacifist
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_country_type = swarm
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				is_xenophobe = yes
				is_xenophobic_isolationists = yes
			}
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_country_type = swarm
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor
				is_open_gestalt = yes
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			any_country = {
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				is_proposing_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_prethoryn
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			any_country = {
				is_galactic_custodian = yes
				is_proposing_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_prethoryn
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			any_country = {
				is_galactic_emperor = yes
				is_proposing_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_prethoryn
			}
		}
	}
}

resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_unbidden = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_emergency_measure"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no

	modifier = {
		resolution_end_game = 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_unbidden_effect_success

		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_unbidden
			set_global_flag = galactic_community_crisis_fighting

			remove_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_prethoryn
			remove_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_contingency
			remove_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_greatkhan
			remove_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_nanites

			set_global_flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_global_flag = extradimensional_invasion_happened
		NOR = {
			has_global_flag = extradimensional_invasion_defeated
			has_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_unbidden
		}
	}

	allow = {
	}

	active = { # Resolution only in effect while this trigger is met
		NOT = { has_global_flag = extradimensional_invasion_defeated }
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_normal
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			has_modifier = prepared_for_the_end
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			any_neighbor_country = {
				OR = {
					is_country_type = extradimensional
					is_country_type = extradimensional_2
					is_country_type = extradimensional_3
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			any_relation = {
				is_in_federation_with = prev
				any_neighbor_country = {
					OR = {
						is_country_type = extradimensional
						is_country_type = extradimensional_2
						is_country_type = extradimensional_3
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_relation = {
				has_defensive_pact = prev
				any_neighbor_country = {
					OR = {
						is_country_type = extradimensional
						is_country_type = extradimensional_2
						is_country_type = extradimensional_3
					}

				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			any_relation = {
				is_rival = prev
				any_neighbor_country = {
					OR = {
						is_country_type = extradimensional
						is_country_type = extradimensional_2
						is_country_type = extradimensional_3
					}

				}
			}
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					OR = {
						is_country_type = extradimensional
						is_country_type = extradimensional_2
						is_country_type = extradimensional_3
					}

				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75

			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					OR = {
						is_country_type = extradimensional
						is_country_type = extradimensional_2
						is_country_type = extradimensional_3
					}
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75

			has_crisis_stage_1 = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2

			has_crisis_stage_3 = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 15

			has_crisis_stage_4 = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 50

			has_ascension_perk = ap_defender_of_the_galaxy
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_philosopher_king
				is_civic_diplomatic_corps = yes
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
				is_civic_inwards_perfection = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			is_militarist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			is_xenophile = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_spiritualist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_spiritualist
		}
		
		# machines and materialists don't understand the shroud very well
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				is_materialist = yes
				is_machine_empire = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_technology = tech_psionic_theory }
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = resolution_galacticstudies_extradimensional_experimentation }
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					OR = {
						is_country_type = extradimensional
						is_country_type = extradimensional_2
						is_country_type = extradimensional_3
					}
				}
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_materialist
				is_civic_materialist = yes
			}
			NOT = { has_technology = tech_psionic_theory }
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = resolution_galacticstudies_extradimensional_experimentation }
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					OR = {
						is_country_type = extradimensional
						is_country_type = extradimensional_2
						is_country_type = extradimensional_3
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_pacifist
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					OR = {
						is_country_type = extradimensional
						is_country_type = extradimensional_2
						is_country_type = extradimensional_3
					}
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				is_xenophobe = yes
				is_xenophobic_isolationists = yes
			}
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					OR = {
						is_country_type = extradimensional
						is_country_type = extradimensional_2
						is_country_type = extradimensional_3
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor
				is_open_gestalt = yes
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = breached_shroud
				has_origin = origin_shroud_pact
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			any_country = {
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				is_proposing_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_unbidden
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			any_country = {
				is_galactic_custodian = yes
				is_proposing_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_unbidden
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			any_country = {
				is_galactic_emperor = yes
				is_proposing_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_unbidden
			}
		}
	}
}

				is_proposing_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_contingency
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			any_country = {
				is_galactic_emperor = yes
				is_proposing_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_contingency
			}
		}
	}

resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_greatkhan = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_emergency_measure"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no

	modifier = {
		resolution_great_khan= 1
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_greatkhan_effect_success

		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_greatkhan
			set_global_flag = galactic_community_crisis_fighting

			remove_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_unbidden
			remove_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_prethoryn
			remove_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_contingency
			remove_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_nanites

			set_global_flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_global_flag = great_khan_announcement
		NOT = { has_global_flag = great_khan_dead }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = galactic_focus_crisis_greatkhan }
	}

	allow = {
	}

	active = { # Resolution only in effect while this trigger is met
		NOT = { has_global_flag = great_khan_dead }
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 0

			is_subject_type = satrapy
			NOT = { has_country_flag = rebelling_satrapy }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 20

			is_subject_type = satrapy
			has_country_flag = rebelling_satrapy
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			any_neighbor_country = {
				is_country_type = awakened_marauders
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 8
			any_relation = {
				is_in_federation_with = prev
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_country_type = awakened_marauders
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			any_relation = {
				has_defensive_pact = prev
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_country_type = awakened_marauders
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			any_relation = {
				is_rival = prev
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_country_type = awakened_marauders
				}
			}
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					is_country_type = awakened_marauders
				}
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 4

			any_neighbor_country = {
				is_subject_type = satrapy
				NOT = { has_country_flag = rebelling_satrapy }
				NOT = { is_rival = prev }
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_philosopher_king
				is_civic_diplomatic_corps = yes
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
				is_civic_inwards_perfection = yes
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			is_militarist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_xenophile = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_pacifist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_pacifist
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				is_xenophobe = yes
				is_xenophobic_isolationists = yes
			}
			NOT = {
				any_neighbor_country = {
					OR = {
						is_country_type = awakened_marauders
						is_subject_type = satrapy
					}
				}
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 6
			OR = {
				has_valid_civic = civic_machine_servitor
				is_open_gestalt = yes
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 3
			any_country = {
				is_part_of_galactic_council = yes
				is_proposing_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_greatkhan
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 4
			any_country = {
				is_galactic_custodian = yes
				is_proposing_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_greatkhan
			}
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 5
			any_country = {
				is_galactic_emperor = yes
				is_proposing_resolution = resolution_galactic_focus_crisis_greatkhan
			}
		}
	}

resolution_galactic_focus_war_in_heaven_support_side_1 = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_emergency_measure"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no

	modifier = {}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_galactic_focus_war_in_heaven_support_side_1_success

		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = galactic_focus_war_in_heaven

			set_global_flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed
			if = {
				limit = { event_target:FirstSleeper = { is_xenophile = yes } }
				set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_xenophile_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { event_target:FirstSleeper = { is_xenophobe = yes } }
				set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_xenophobe_supremacist_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { event_target:FirstSleeper = { is_materialist = yes } }
				set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_materialist_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { event_target:FirstSleeper = { is_spiritualist = yes } }
				set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_spiritualist_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_global_flag = war_in_heaven_ongoing
		NOT = { has_global_flag = galactic_focus_war_in_heaven }
		exists = event_target:SecondSleeper
	}

	allow = {
	}

	active = { # Resolution only in effect while this trigger is met
		has_global_flag = war_in_heaven_ongoing
		exists = event_target:FirstSleeper
		exists = event_target:SecondSleeper
	}

	breach = {
		NAND = {
			exists = overlord
			has_overlord = event_target:FirstSleeper
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		base = @resolution_weight_normal

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			exists = overlord
			has_overlord = event_target:FirstSleeper
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			exists = overlord
			has_overlord = event_target:SecondSleeper
		}
	}
}

resolution_galactic_focus_war_in_heaven_denounce_both = {

		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}

	triggered_modifier = {
		potential = {
			has_global_flag = war_in_heaven_ongoing
			OR = {
				NOT = { exists = overlord }
				overlord = {
					NOR = {
						is_same_value = event_target:FirstSleeper

					}

resolution_tiyanki_conservation_act = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_tiyanki_preservation"

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
	}

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_denounce
		}
	}
	target = no

	modifier = {
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_tiyanki_conservation_act_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_xenophobe_supremacist_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		NOR = {
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_tiyanki_pest_control"
			has_global_flag = tiyanki_extinct
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOR = {
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_tiyanki_conservation_act"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_amoeba_conservation_act"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_crystal_conservation_act"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_space_cloud_conservation_act"
				is_active_resolution = "resolution_drone_conservation_act"
			}
		}
	}

	active = { # Resolution only in effect while this trigger is met
		NOT = { has_global_flag = tiyanki_extinct }
	}

	breach = {
		has_country_flag = resolution_breached_killed_tiyanki
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			is_xenophile = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_pacifist = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_pacifist
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_militarist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_civic_militarist = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			OR = {
				is_materialist = yes
				is_auth_corporate = yes
				is_civic_mining_guilds = yes
				has_valid_civic = civic_corporate_dominion
				has_valid_civic = civic_machine_assimilator
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_origin = origin_natural_hunters
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			OR = {
				is_civic_environmentalist = yes
				has_valid_civic = civic_hive_empath
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			owner_species = { has_trait = eco_trait_clean }
		}
		
		modifier = {

		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5

		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_xenophobic_isolationists = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_pacifist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_pacifist
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_militarist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_civic_militarist = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				is_materialist = yes
				is_auth_corporate = yes
				is_civic_mining_guilds = yes
				has_valid_civic = civic_corporate_dominion

			OR = {
				is_civic_environmentalist = yes

		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			owner_species = { has_trait = eco_trait_dirty }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_xenophile = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_origin = origin_amoeba
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			in_breach_of = resolution_tiyanki_conservation_act
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_federation_ally = {
				NOT = {
					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }
				}
				in_breach_of = resolution_tiyanki_conservation_act
			}
		}
	}

		}

		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = galcom.103 }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_xenophile_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_pacifist_outraged_gc days = 7200 }

			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		NOR = {
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_tiyanki_conservation_act"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_amoeba_conservation_act"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_crystal_conservation_act"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_space_cloud_conservation_act"
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_drone_conservation_act"
			has_global_flag = tiyanki_extinct
		}
	}

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_already_active"
			NOT = { is_active_resolution = "resolution_tiyanki_pest_control" }
		}
	}

	active = { # Resolution only in effect while this trigger is met
		NOT = { has_global_flag = tiyanki_extinct }
	}

	breach = {
		has_country_flag = resolution_breached_tiyanki_inside_borders
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_xenophobic_isolationists = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			is_xenophobe = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_pacifist = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_pacifist
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_militarist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_civic_militarist = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			OR = {
				is_materialist = yes
				is_auth_corporate = yes
				is_civic_mining_guilds = yes
				has_valid_civic = civic_corporate_dominion
				has_valid_civic = civic_machine_assimilator

resolution_repeal_crystal_conservation_act = {
	icon = "GFX_repeal_blue"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_denounce
		}
	}

	target = no

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_repeal_crystal_conservation_act_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			pass_resolution = resolution_amoeba_conservation_act
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_galactic_community_member = yes
					has_modifier = pacified_crystals
					NOR = {
						is_xenophile = yes
						is_pacifist = yes
						has_civic = civic_machine_servitor
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = diploevent.19 }
			}
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_ecology_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_xenophile_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_pacifist_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_ecology_repeal days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		is_active_resolution = "resolution_crystal_conservation_act"
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_xenophobic_isolationists = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			is_xenophobe = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			is_pacifist = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_pacifist
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_militarist = yes
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_militarist
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_civic_militarist = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			OR = {
				is_materialist = yes
				is_auth_corporate = yes
				is_civic_mining_guilds = yes
				has_valid_civic = civic_corporate_dominion
				has_valid_civic = civic_machine_assimilator
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 100
			has_origin = origin_natural_hunters
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			OR = {
				is_civic_environmentalist = yes
				is_civic_machine_servitor = yes
				has_valid_civic = civic_hive_empath
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.75
			owner_species = { has_trait = eco_trait_clean }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.2
			owner_species = { has_trait = eco_trait_dirty }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_xenophile = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 10
			in_breach_of = resolution_crystal_conservation_act
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_federation_ally = {
				NOT = {
					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }
				}
				in_breach_of = resolution_crystal_conservation_act
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_origin = origin_amoeba
		}
	}
}

			is_xenophobe = no
		}
		modifier = {

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			any_federation_ally = {
				NOT = {
					federation = { has_federation_type = hegemony_federation }
				}
				in_breach_of = resolution_drone_conservation_act
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_civic_mining_guilds = yes
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

		custom_tooltip = resolution_galactic_market_ban_sentient_organic_slave_trade_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = organic_slave_trade_banned_flag
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_authoritarian_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = faction_xenophobe_supremacist_outraged_gc days = 7200 }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
		has_megacorp = yes
		NOT = {
			is_active_resolution = "resolution_galactic_market_ban_sentient_organic_slave_trade"
			has_global_flag = organic_slave_trade_banned_flag
		}
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_xenophile = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_egalitarian = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			NOT = { has_ai_personality_behaviour = slaver }
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_egalitarian
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophile
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_xenophobe = yes
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_authoritarian = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_ai_personality_behaviour = slaver
			OR = {
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_authoritarian
				has_ethic = ethic_fanatic_xenophobe
			}
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			NOT = { has_ai_personality_behaviour = slaver }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			has_ai_personality_behaviour = slaver
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_slaver = yes
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			is_civic_slaver_guilds = yes
		}

resolution_galactic_market_relocate = {
	icon = "GFX_resolution_relocate_galactic_market"

	resources = {
		category = resolutions
		cost = {
			influence = @resolution_cost_t1
		}
	}
	target = no

	allow = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			fail_text = "resolution_galactic_market_relocate_trigger_fail"
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = "resolution_galactic_market_relocated_recently"
			}
		}
	}

	effect = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		custom_tooltip = resolution_galactic_market_relocate_effect_success
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = galcom.64 }

			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_passed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }

			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_passed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}

			set_timed_global_flag = { flag = resolution_galactic_market_relocated_recently days = 18000 }
		}
	}

	fail_effects = {
		hidden_effect = { add_modifier = { modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight days = 2200 } }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_timed_country_flag = { flag = galactic_community_resolution_failed_general days = @resolution_flag_timer }
			add_modifier = {
				modifier = resolution_failed_diplomatic_weight
				days = 2200
			}
		}
	}

	modifier = {
	}

	potential = {
		has_federations_dlc = yes
		has_megacorp = yes
		has_global_flag = galactic_market_founded
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = ongoing_market_relocation_nomination
		}
		NOT = { has_modifier = galactic_market_founder }
		is_gestalt = no
		is_homicidal = no
	}

	ai_weight = {
		weight = @resolution_weight_disliked

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			has_modifier = galactic_market_founder
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			any_federation_ally = {
				has_modifier = galactic_market_founder
			}
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_gestalt = no
			has_resource = { type = influence amount < 400 }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			is_gestalt = no
			has_resource = { type = influence amount > 700 }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 2
			is_auth_corporate = yes
			NOT = { has_modifier = galactic_market_founder }
		}

		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			has_ai_personality = peaceful_traders
			NOT = { has_modifier = galactic_market_founder }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			has_ai_personality = ruthless_capitalists
			NOT = { has_modifier = galactic_market_founder }
		}
		
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.5
			is_gestalt = yes
		}
	}
}
